<div id="review_191031445" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/191031445" />
    <a title="Hillary Hunt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4660282-hillary-hunt"><img alt="Hillary Hunt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372101188p2/4660282.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/191031445?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hillary Hunt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hillary Hunt" href="/user/show/4660282-hillary-hunt">Hillary Hunt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12190788-the-near-witch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4660282-hillary-hunt?shelf=fem-fantasy">fem-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4660282-hillary-hunt?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer191031445" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15648057548930198552">Victoria Schwab's writing will rope you in with its lyrical loveliness, I will say that. But the actual plot of the Near Witch is rather ho-hum. After all the swooning reviews I read for this one, I was expecting more. Here's why it didn't capture my fancy:<br/><br/>Not much suspense. You pretty much know what's going on the whole time, there are no surprises. <br/><br/>The book is written in first person, from the pov of Lexi. And yet her character came across as very vague and nondescript. I did not understand wh</span>
  <span id="freeText15648057548930198552" style="display:none">Victoria Schwab's writing will rope you in with its lyrical loveliness, I will say that. But the actual plot of the Near Witch is rather ho-hum. After all the swooning reviews I read for this one, I was expecting more. Here's why it didn't capture my fancy:<br /><br />Not much suspense. You pretty much know what's going on the whole time, there are no surprises. <br /><br />The book is written in first person, from the pov of Lexi. And yet her character came across as very vague and nondescript. I did not understand where her drive came from. <br /><br />The romance was flimsy and unsupported by the story. They go from strangers to devoted to each other over night. Blink and you'll miss it. <br /><br />The stakes were too low. You pretty much know there's no bite in this book when you're reading it. Makes you care less.<br /><br />The whole plot just felt undercooked. There just wasn't a lot there. The story felt....small. And I don't mean in length, I mean in depth and development. I wanted more. I wanted more of who Lexi was, who Cole was, why they were attracted to each other, more suspense, more fear. I wanted there to be more explanation of why Lexi was so compelled to sneak out every night. I wanted Otto to do more than just huff and puff. I wanted a compelling reason to care or worry about the characters. But like I said, it stayed small, thin.....I don't know how else to describe it. <br /><br />So that all may sound harsh, but honest to goodness I think Victoria Schwab is a wonderful tailor of words. But that was not enough to make this book captivating to me. If you want to best show off a well tailored suit, you need a good frame to hang it on.<br /><br />My favorite bit:<br /><br />"My Father used to say that change is like a garden.<br /><br />It doesn't come up overnight, unless you are a witch. Things have to be planted and tended, and most of all, the ground has to be right. He said the people of Near had the wrong dirt, and that's why they resisted change so much, the way roots resist hard earth. He said if you could just break through, there was good soil there, down deep."<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15648057548930198552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3306188710" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja Ingrid" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja Ingrid" href="/user/show/22024209-maja-ingrid">Maja Ingrid</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781789091144" href="/book/show/44638436-the-near-witch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22024209-maja-ingrid?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22024209-maja-ingrid?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3306188710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12067538171960820081">This is V.E Schwab’s first published work, which shows. In a good way, because it shows just how much she’s developed as a writer and story-teller. <br/><br/>It annoyed me a little I learned so little about the world this was set in. We barely even learn much about the village Near. We learn a little about social structures, how women are supposed to to womanly stuff and men do men stuff. But I had some issues trying to create a picture of how the world looked and functioned in broader strokes. <br/><br/>The story </span>
  <span id="freeText12067538171960820081" style="display:none">This is V.E Schwab’s first published work, which shows. In a good way, because it shows just how much she’s developed as a writer and story-teller. <br /><br />It annoyed me a little I learned so little about the world this was set in. We barely even learn much about the village Near. We learn a little about social structures, how women are supposed to to womanly stuff and men do men stuff. But I had some issues trying to create a picture of how the world looked and functioned in broader strokes. <br /><br />The story is familiar, because it’s been done before. Children going missing in the dead of night. (new, if there is one) person being blamed for it. Search for the guilty one. It’s short and simple. But is still atmospheric at parts. <br /><br />Schwab’s writing has also definitely improved miles since this book. I wasn’t to fond of the writing style in this one. I am also not fond of first person present tense and it didn’t really for me in this one. It doesn’t run smoothly for me. <br /></span>

<div id="review_136911450" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/136911450" />
    <a title="Patricia Riley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4443893-patricia-riley"><img alt="Patricia Riley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451687313p2/4443893.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/136911450?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patricia Riley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patricia Riley" href="/user/show/4443893-patricia-riley">Patricia Riley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4443893-patricia-riley?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer136911450" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12374577552140600326">I was lucky enough to get a ARC of The Near Witch and it turned out to be, by a mile, my favorite of the (many) books I read in 2010! Within two weeks of getting it, I read it twice! As I read it again today to celebrate it's release it will be the 6th time I've read it! Suffice to say this book managed to do two things that I have not had a book do in a very, very long time: <br/><br/>1) It so completely drew me in and entangled me in the world of the story that if someone had jumped out in front of me w</span>
  <span id="freeText12374577552140600326" style="display:none">I was lucky enough to get a ARC of The Near Witch and it turned out to be, by a mile, my favorite of the (many) books I read in 2010! Within two weeks of getting it, I read it twice! As I read it again today to celebrate it's release it will be the 6th time I've read it! Suffice to say this book managed to do two things that I have not had a book do in a very, very long time: <br /><br />1) It so completely drew me in and entangled me in the world of the story that if someone had jumped out in front of me while I was reading and shouted "Quick! Tell me where you are?" it would have taken me a good minute or two to come back to reality and read adjust my brain to the point where I could answer correctly; and <br /><br />2) at LEAST twice book had a moment so emotionally tense that I literally jumped up from my seat and didn't realize I was standing until the tense moment had passed. <br /><br />This book is brilliant and you should read it as soon as you possibly can! Fair warning though, you probably want to set aside enough time to read the whole thing... this book will haunt you (in a fabulous OMG-what-is-going-to-happen-next kind of way) if you try to put it down before you finish it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12374577552140600326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2840467990" />
    <a title="Ashley Daviau" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35915119-ashley-daviau"><img alt="Ashley Daviau" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599784716p2/35915119.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2840467990?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashley Daviau" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashley Daviau" href="/user/show/35915119-ashley-daviau">Ashley Daviau</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2840467990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16808377501969429596">This was such a beautiful and haunting read, I was instantly hooked and dragged into this stunning story. The only reason I didn’t binge read it in one sitting is because I was reading along with a friend. I can’t believe this is Schwab’s first novel, it’s kind of mind blowing! She just knocks it out of the park every single damn time. It reads like a beautifully eerie fairy tale and I couldn’t have loved it more. It’s just so deliciously creepy, it made my little black heart so happy!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2791447863" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2791447863" />
    <a title="Julie Zantopoulos" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51094260-julie-zantopoulos"><img alt="Julie Zantopoulos" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1503178209p2/51094260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2791447863?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie Zantopoulos" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie Zantopoulos" href="/user/show/51094260-julie-zantopoulos">Julie Zantopoulos</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781789092165" href="/book/show/43404078-the-near-witch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/51094260-julie-zantopoulos?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/51094260-julie-zantopoulos?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2791447863" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15036931431070598883"><i>"Fear is a strange thing, it has the power to make people close their eyes, turn away. Nothing good grows out of fear."</i><br/><br/>Near is a cozy town bordering the moors, the woods, and the land where nothing grows. The setting of this novel is a character all its own, it's rich and alive. I adore the small-town feel, the town's lore and history, it's ghost stories and traditions. Just like most small towns, they have some warped ideas/ideals and our main character Lexi is questioning them all. <br/><br/><i>"Change is </i></span>
  <span id="freeText15036931431070598883" style="display:none"><i>"Fear is a strange thing, it has the power to make people close their eyes, turn away. Nothing good grows out of fear."</i><br /><br />Near is a cozy town bordering the moors, the woods, and the land where nothing grows. The setting of this novel is a character all its own, it's rich and alive. I adore the small-town feel, the town's lore and history, it's ghost stories and traditions. Just like most small towns, they have some warped ideas/ideals and our main character Lexi is questioning them all. <br /><br /><i>"Change is like a garden. It doesn't come up overnight. THings have to be planted and tended, and most of all, the ground has to be right."</i><br /><br />Her father went missing, her uncle Otto has taken over responsibility for their household because her mother has never quite been the same since her father left. Her sister Wren is fighting the urge to run off into the Moors and follow her friends that have gone missing. But is it the Near Witch back to exact revenge or the new boy that showed up the night the first kid went missing that is the blame? <br /><br /><i>"Believing and knowing are different things. ... Knowing and proving are different things."</i><br /><br />Lexi knows that Cole didn't hurt the kids and not just because his touch sets her heart racing but because he's been helping her at night to hunt for the children. But in a town where the men rule and they want her sitting safely inside, Lexi is in danger. A possessive town friend, Tyler, doesn't like her sneaking off at night but town witches, Magda and Deska, are doing what they can to aid Lexi and Cole. Will they be able to save the children in time? <br /><br />For a debut novel, this was really magical and atmospheric. It is so different from Schwab's later work but I really enjoyed it. <br /><br />TW: arson, violence, attempted murder, haunting, murder, sexual assault, and kidnapping.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15036931431070598883" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2623296715" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2623296715" />
    <a title="Rachel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/642255-rachel"><img alt="Rachel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579016628p2/642255.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2623296715?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel" href="/user/show/642255-rachel">Rachel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781789091120" href="/book/show/42370636-the-near-witch">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2623296715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2216589848941900571">The Near Witch reads like a classic fairytale with roots embedded in the tale of the Near Witch who could control the elements and grow magical gardens. The tale the children have been taught though, isn't entirely accurate, and when a mysterious stranger comes to town, and children begin disappearing from their beds, the menfolk go on a literal witch hunt, and 16-year-old Lexi needs to find the missing children before the men hunt the wrong person.<br/><br/>I loved that this incorporated a mystery elemen</span>
  <span id="freeText2216589848941900571" style="display:none">The Near Witch reads like a classic fairytale with roots embedded in the tale of the Near Witch who could control the elements and grow magical gardens. The tale the children have been taught though, isn't entirely accurate, and when a mysterious stranger comes to town, and children begin disappearing from their beds, the menfolk go on a literal witch hunt, and 16-year-old Lexi needs to find the missing children before the men hunt the wrong person.<br><br>I loved that this incorporated a mystery element with old town legends, the classic witch hunt storyline, and a bit of magic. It reminded me greatly of the Johnny Depp era, Sleepy Hollow, in a good way.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1562595081ra/27791577.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had some trouble latching on in the beginning, I think because it has a slow start and I listened to this as audiobook, and as well-spoken and eloquent as the reader was, her inflection was slightly off? She didn't come down at the end of a sentence, and I found it hard to get into. If you're having trouble on audio, I might suggest the physical book.<br><br>Regardless, once I muddled through the intro and the reading, I was hooked. V.E. Schwab was clearly a gifted writer from a young age. This is impressive as a second or third book, inspiring as a debut. If you enjoyed her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20764879.A_Gathering_of_Shadows__Shades_of_Magic___2_" title="A Gathering of Shadows (Shades of Magic, #2) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a> series, you will enjoy this too. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2216589848941900571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tWZGoydzuFcUC6Tf7xIkLFe1pa2UvFo3YiutgDs1HRI7xG3iJz4ycRwd987Pz5Bjbg6nMIlSxYth/OhcJZNhzQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('njPtsIWkLjyz49JndthpankgFI/HYoAkw/eLLlxaBqgQkcbxhemkGrv1gXZWBd0lQJsWEtqMH5jAIM7yQvx6dw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15355927971670987350">Victoria is the product of a British mother, a Beverly Hills father, and a southern upbringing. Because of this, she has been known to say "tom-ah-toes," "like," and "y'all."<br/><br/>She also tells stories.<br/><br/>She loves fairy tales, and folklore, and stories that make her wonder if the world is really as it seems. <br/></span>
